NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE

739

PUBLIC NOTICES

ULTIMA DENTAL LAB PRIVATE LIMITED
Regd. Off: 8C, Ram Mansion, 392, Pantheon Road, Egmore, Chennai-600 008.
Pursuant to Section 485 of the Companies Act, 1956, notice is hereby given that at the Extraordinary
General Meeting of the Company held on 25th February 2014, the following Special Resolution was passed unanimously to
Voluntarily wind up the Company.
“RESOLVED THAT the Company be Wound Up Voluntarily, Pursuant to Section 488 (1)(b) of the Companies Act,
1956 as Members’ Voluntary Liquidation.
RESOLVED FURTHER THAT Mr. C. Ramasubramaniam, Practising Company Secretary, Managing Partner CR &
Associates, Chennai be and is hereby appointed as Liquidator for the purpose of such Winding Up and that he be remunerated
Rs.1,00,000/- (Rupees one lakh only) as Professional Fees towards Winding Up of the Company.
RESOLVED FURTHER THAT the Liquidator be and is hereby authorized to exercise all or any of the powers given
under Clauses (i) to (iv) of sub-section (2) of Section 457 of the Companies Act, 1956".

For ultima Dental Lab Private Limited,

Chennai,
7th March 2014.

K. ARULKANNAN,
Director.

FORM No. 151
(See Rule 315)
